  19 /*
  20  * ALGORITHM DESCRIPTION:
  21  *
  22  *   Approximation formula:
  23  *   erfc(x)~erfc(x0)-2/sqrt(pi)*exp(-x0^2)*D*[1+(x0*D)*p1(x0*D)+D^2*p3(x0*D)+D^4*p5(x0*D)+D^6*p7(x0*D)]
  24  *     D = x - x0
  25  *     erfc(x0) and 2/sqrt(pi)*exp(-x0^2)/(2*x0) are tabulated
  26  *
  27  *
  28  */
  29 
  30 /* Offsets for data table __svml_derfc_data_internal
  31  */
  32 #define _erfc_tbl                       0
  33 #define _AbsMask                        55808
  34 #define _MaxThreshold                   55824
  35 #define _SgnMask                        55840
  36 #define _TwoM128                        55856
  37 #define _SRound                         55872
  38 #define _poly1_0                        55888
  39 #define _poly1_1                        55904
  40 #define _poly3_0                        55920
  41 #define _poly3_1                        55936
  42 #define _poly5_0                        55952
  43 #define _poly5_1                        55968
  44 #define _poly1_2                        55984
  45 #define _poly3_2                        56000
  46 #define _poly5_2                        56016
  47 #define _poly1_3                        56032
  48 #define _poly3_3                        56048
  49 #define _poly5_3                        56064
  50 #define _poly1_4                        56080
  51 #define _poly3_4                        56096
  52 #define _poly1_5                        56112
  53 #define _poly3_5                        56128
  54 #define _poly3_6                        56144
  55 #define _poly1_6                        56160
  56 #define _poly1_7                        56176
  57 #define _UF_Threshold                   56192
  58 #define _TwoP128                        56208
  59 
  60 #include <sysdep.h>
  61 
  62         .text
  63     .section .text.sse4,"ax",@progbits
  64 ENTRY(_ZGVbN2v_erfc_sse4)
  65         subq      $72, %rsp
  66         cfi_def_cfa_offset(80)
  67         movaps    %xmm0, %xmm4
  68         movups    _AbsMask+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm2
  69 
  70 /* vector gather: erfc_h(x0), (erfc_l(x0), 2/sqrt(pi)*exp(-x0^2)) */
  71         lea       __svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %rcx
  72         andps     %xmm4, %xmm2
  73 
  74 /*
  75  * erfc(27.25) underflows to 0
  76  * can compute all results in the main path
  77  */
  78         minpd     _MaxThreshold+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm2
  79         movups    _SRound+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm6
  80         movaps    %xmm6, %xmm8
  81         addpd     %xmm2, %xmm8
  82         movups    _TwoM128+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm0
  83         movaps    %xmm8, %xmm1
  84         maxpd     %xmm0, %xmm2
  85         subpd     %xmm6, %xmm1
  86         subpd     %xmm1, %xmm2
  87         mulpd     %xmm2, %xmm1
  88 
  89 /* Start polynomial evaluation */
  90         movups    _poly1_0+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
  91 
  92 /* Diff^2 */
  93         movaps    %xmm2, %xmm15
  94         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm13
  95         mulpd     %xmm2, %xmm15
  96         addpd     _poly1_1+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
  97         movups    _poly3_0+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm11
  98 
  99 /* T^2 */
 100         movaps    %xmm1, %xmm14
 101         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm11
 102         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm13
 103         addpd     _poly3_1+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm11
 104         addpd     _poly1_2+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
 105         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm14
 106         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm11
 107         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm13
 108         addpd     _poly3_2+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm11
 109         addpd     _poly1_3+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
 110         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm11
 111         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm13
 112         addpd     _poly3_3+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm11
 113         addpd     _poly1_4+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
 114         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm11
 115         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm13
 116         addpd     _poly3_4+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm11
 117         addpd     _poly1_5+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
 118         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm11
 119         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm13
 120         addpd     _poly3_5+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm11
 121         addpd     _poly1_6+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
 122         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm11
 123         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm13
 124         movups    _poly5_0+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm12
 125         psllq     $4, %xmm8
 126         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm12
 127         addpd     _poly1_7+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm13
 128         addpd     _poly5_1+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm12
 129         movd      %xmm8, %eax
 130         mulpd     %xmm13, %xmm14
 131         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm12
 132         addpd     _poly5_2+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm12
 133         mulpd     %xmm1, %xmm12
 134         addpd     _poly5_3+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm12
 135 
 136 /* P5 = P5 + D2*P07 */
 137         mulpd     %xmm15, %xmm12
 138         addpd     _poly3_6+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm12
 139         addpd     %xmm11, %xmm12
 140         mulpd     %xmm12, %xmm15
 141         pshufd    $2, %xmm8, %xmm9
 142         movd      %xmm9, %edx
 143         movups    _TwoP128+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm5
 144         movups    _SgnMask+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm7
 145         movaps    %xmm5, %xmm3
 146         movslq    %eax, %rax
 147         andps     %xmm4, %xmm7
 148         movslq    %edx, %rdx
 149         orps      %xmm7, %xmm3
 150         subpd     %xmm1, %xmm15
 151         subpd     %xmm5, %xmm3
 152         addpd     %xmm14, %xmm15
 153         movups    (%rcx,%rax), %xmm5
 154 
 155 /* Special arguments (for flags only) */
 156         movaps    %xmm4, %xmm1
 157         movups    (%rcx,%rdx), %xmm10
 158         movaps    %xmm5, %xmm6
 159         unpckhpd  %xmm10, %xmm5
 160 
 161 /* 2^(-128) with sign of input */
 162         orps      %xmm7, %xmm0
 163 
 164 /* EXP_X0H *= Diff */
 165         mulpd     %xmm2, %xmm5
 166         cmpltpd   _UF_Threshold+__svml_derfc_data_internal(%rip), %xmm1
 167 
 168 /* EXP_x0H*Diff*(1+P1) */
 169         mulpd     %xmm5, %xmm15
 170 
 171 /* combine and get argument value range mask */
 172         movmskpd  %xmm1, %edx
 173         unpcklpd  %xmm10, %xmm6
 174         addpd     %xmm15, %xmm5
 175 
 176 /* erfc(|_VARG1|) = erfc_h(x0) - P1 */
 177         subpd     %xmm5, %xmm6
 178         addpd     %xmm6, %xmm3
 179         notl      %edx
 180         mulpd     %xmm3, %xmm0
 181         andl      $3, %edx
 182 
 183 /* Go to special inputs processing branch */
 184         jne       L(SPECIAL_VALUES_BRANCH)
 185                                 # LOE rbx rbp r12 r13 r14 r15 edx xmm0 xmm4
 186 
 187 /* Restore registers
 188  * and exit the function
 189  */
 190 
 191 L(EXIT):
 192         addq      $72, %rsp
 193         cfi_def_cfa_offset(8)
 194         ret
 195         cfi_def_cfa_offset(80)
 196 
 197 /* Branch to process
 198  * special inputs
 199  */
 200 
 201 L(SPECIAL_VALUES_BRANCH):
 202         movups    %xmm4, 32(%rsp)
 203         movups    %xmm0, 48(%rsp)
 204                                 # LOE rbx rbp r12 r13 r14 r15 edx xmm0
 205 
 206         xorl      %eax, %eax
 207         movq      %r12, 16(%rsp)
 208         cfi_offset(12, -64)
 209         movl      %eax, %r12d
 210         movq      %r13, 8(%rsp)
 211         cfi_offset(13, -72)
 212         movl      %edx, %r13d
 213         movq      %r14, (%rsp)
 214         cfi_offset(14, -80)
 215                                 # LOE rbx rbp r15 r12d r13d
 216 
 217 /* Range mask
 218  * bits check
 219  */
 220 
 221 L(RANGEMASK_CHECK):
 222         btl       %r12d, %r13d
 223 
 224 /* Call scalar math function */
 225         jc        L(SCALAR_MATH_CALL)
 226                                 # LOE rbx rbp r15 r12d r13d
 227 
 228 /* Special inputs
 229  * processing loop
 230  */
 231 
 232 L(SPECIAL_VALUES_LOOP):
 233         incl      %r12d
 234         cmpl      $2, %r12d
 235 
 236 /* Check bits in range mask */
 237         jl        L(RANGEMASK_CHECK)
 238                                 # LOE rbx rbp r15 r12d r13d
 239 
 240         movq      16(%rsp), %r12
 241         cfi_restore(12)
 242         movq      8(%rsp), %r13
 243         cfi_restore(13)
 244         movq      (%rsp), %r14
 245         cfi_restore(14)
 246         movups    48(%rsp), %xmm0
 247 
 248 /* Go to exit */
 249         jmp       L(EXIT)
 250         cfi_offset(12, -64)
 251         cfi_offset(13, -72)
 252         cfi_offset(14, -80)
 253                                 # LOE rbx rbp r12 r13 r14 r15 xmm0
 254 
 255 /* Scalar math fucntion call
 256  * to process special input
 257  */
 258 
 259 L(SCALAR_MATH_CALL):
 260         movl      %r12d, %r14d
 261         movsd     32(%rsp,%r14,8), %xmm0
 262         call      erfc@PLT
 263                                 # LOE rbx rbp r14 r15 r12d r13d xmm0
 264 
 265         movsd     %xmm0, 48(%rsp,%r14,8)
 266 
 267 /* Process special inputs in loop */
 268         jmp       L(SPECIAL_VALUES_LOOP)
 269                                 # LOE rbx rbp r15 r12d r13d
 270 END(_ZGVbN2v_erfc_sse4)
 271 
 272         .section .rodata, "a"
 273         .align 16
